applies to all incident management tows performed by tow truck companies inside the corporate boundaries of the city as amended from time to time  2112010 definitions the following words terms and phrases when used in this chapter shall have the meanings ascribed to them in this section except where the context clearly indicates a different meaning accidentrelated tow means any incident management tow of a vehicle by a towing company in which the tow truck is summoned by the city police department because of a traffic accident consent tow means any tow of a motor vehicle in which the tow truck is summoned by the owner or operator of the vehicle or by a person who has possession custody or control of the vehicle the term consent tow does not include an incident management tow or a private property tow incident management tow means any tow of a vehicle by a towing company in which the tow truck is summoned by the city police department because of a traffic accident or to an incident the phrase incident management tow includes an accidentrelated tow and a nonaccident related tow nonconsent tow means any tow of a motor vehicle that is not a consent tow including 1 an incident management tow  and 2 a private property tow nonaccidentrelated tow means any incident management tow of a vehicle by a towing company in which the tow truck is summoned by the city police department for reasons other than a traffic accident towing company means an individual association corporation or other legal entity that controls operates or directs the operation of one or more tow trucks over a public roadway in this state but does not include a political subdivision of the state  2112010 towing rotation list a city police department the city police department is responsible for establishing maintaining and supervising the administration of a towing rotation list for tow truck companies capable of responding to requests by the city police department for incident management tows within the corporate boundaries of the city within 20 minutes of receiving a request 24 hours per day seven days per week the city police department is authorized to adopt administrative policies consistent with this chapter for the purpose of implementing this chapter b delegation of administration of towing rotation list all tow truck companies placed on the towing rotation list in accordance with this chapter are hereby charged with the responsibility of adopting and administering a central dispatching procedure in a manner approved by the city police chief or designee the central dispatching procedure must be administered at no cost to the city or the city police department and must ensure consistent rotation of tow truck companies on the towing rotation list c preapproved central dispatching procedure default procedure unless the city police chief or designee approves an alternative central dispatching procedure the central dispatching procedure effective at the time of adoption of the ordinance from which this chapter is derived is as follows all tow truck companies on the towing rotation list shall agree to purchase one cellular telephone to be shared among one another at their own collective cost on  the cellular phone shall be initially placed in the possession of one towing company who shall maintain possession of the cellular phone until  pm the following monday when it shall be tendered to the next towing company on the towing rotation list the cell phone shall then be passed from towing company to towing company in consecutive order according to the towing rotation list on a weekly basis beginning at  pm monday and ending at  pm the following monday the city police department shall make all requests for incident management tows by calling the telephone number assigned to the cellular phone whichever towing company is in possession of the cellular phone is responsible for responding to the city police departments request for an incident management tow d application for placement on towing rotation list the city police chief may only place a towing company on the towing rotation list who 1 submits a written application to the city police department to be placed on the towing rotation list  2 states in its application that the towing company is capable of responding to requests for incident management tows within 20 minutes of receiving a request 24 hours per day seven days per week  and 3 provides in the application one central phone number that the city police chief may use to contact the applicant 24 hours per day seven days per week and one cell phone number that the city police chief may use to contact the applicant the city police chief is authorized to adopt a mandatory form for the referenced application the city police department must require applicants to execute an acknowledgment and consent of conditions for placement on the towing rotation list detailing the conditions imposed by this chapter prior to placing any applicant on the towing rotation list e voluntary removal from towing rotation list the city police department may remove any towing company from the towing rotation list upon receiving a written request from the towing company to be removed from the towing rotation list f involuntary removal from towing rotation list 1 the city police department may remove the towing company from the towing rotation list if the city police department determines that a towing company on the towing rotation list has a failed to respond to requests for incident management tows on three or more occasions  b failed to follow the central dispatching procedure approved by the city police department  c failed to follow other administrative polices established by the city police department  d failed to maintain or update licenses required by state law  e failed to comply with standards required by state law  or f failed to maintain insurance required by state law 2 the city police chief must send any towing company removed from the towing rotation list notice of the city police departments removal decision within five days after the date the towing company is removed from the towing rotation list a appeal of removal decision any towing company involuntarily removed from the towing rotation list may appeal the city police departments removal decision to the city council by filing with the city secretary within 14 calendar days from the date the towing company received notice of removal a written request for a hearing before the city council upon receipt of a request for hearing the city secretary shall schedule the hearing for the date of the next regularly scheduled meeting of the city council if a towing company fails to request a hearing before the city council in accordance with this section the towing company is precluded from filing a new application for placement on the towing rotation list for one year from the date the towing company received notice of removal b city council determination the city council in its sole and absolute discretion may affirm or reverse the decision of the city police department the city councils decision is a final legislative decision and each towing company acknowledges by its participation that the councils decision cannot be appealed to any court of law g independent contractors all tow truck companies on the towing rotation list are independent contractors with respect to the city and shall not be deemed to be employees or agents of the city h insurance any towing company on the towing rotation list must maintain liability insurance in accordance with state law i indemnity each towing company on the towing rotation list must as a condition to being placed on towing rotation list indemnify and hold the city harmless from any and all claims or causes of action asserted against the city that arise out of or relate to the towing companys performance of any acts authorized by this chapter as a condition for participation each towing company must provide the city proof of insurance and list the city as an additional insured and file a copy of proof of insurance with the citys police chief or designee  2112010 fee schedule a the city council is authorized to impose and amend fees that may be charged for in connection with performing incident management tows within the citys which term includes the authorized agent of a parent of the minor b defenses it is a defense to prosecution of this section that the minor was 1 accompanied by another minor whose parent was present  2 in a motor vehicle with another minor whose parent was present  3 engaged in any employment activity official school activity at a public school and pursuant to any school activities or going to or from any employment or school activity without any detour or stop  4 involved in an emergency  5 attending any official school religious or other recreational activity supervised by adults and sponsored by any civic organization political organization or religious organization or going to or returning home from any such activity  6 engaged in exercising their rights under the united states constitution providing for the free exercise of religion freedom of speech right of assembly or petition to the government  7 engaged in an errand for the minors parent and continuing on such errand collection or in any duly licensed disposal facility b it shall be unlawful for any person to place or dispose of in any manner any litter along or near or on any land adjoining any public road or highway or ditch except in a properly maintained landfill operated by the city or licensed by the city council 02   prevention of scattering persons placing litter in public receptacles or in authorized private receptacles shall do so in such manner as to prevent litter from being carried or deposited by the elements upon any public place or private premises 03   upsetting or tampering with receptacles no person shall upset or tamper with a public or private receptacle designed or used for the deposit of litter or cause or permit its contents to be deposited or strewn in or upon any public place or private premises 04   sidewalks and alleys to be kept clear the person owning occupying or in control of any public place or private premises shall keep the sidewalks and alleys adjacent thereto free of litter 05   owner to maintain private premises a the owner or person in control of any private premises shall at all times maintain the premises free of litter b the owner or person in control of private premises shall if public receptacles are unavailable maintain authorized private receptacles for collection in such a manner that litter will be prevented from being carried or deposited by the elements upon any public place or private premises 06   littering from vehicles or aircraft a no person while the operator of or passenger in a vehicle shall deposit litter upon any public place or private premises b no person shall drive or move any loaded or partly loaded truck or other vehicle within the city unless such vehicle is so constructed or loaded as to prevent any part of its load contents or litter from being blown or deposited upon any public place or private premises nor shall any person drive or move any vehicle or truck within the city the wheels or tires of which carry onto or deposit in any public place or private premises mud dirt sticky substances litter or foreign matter of any kind c no person shall transport junk refuse or garbage in any manner over and upon any street alley road parkway park drive or public highway in such a manner that it is strewn upon and along such street alley road or public highway d no person in any aircraft shall throw out drop or deposit any litter within the city 07   litter in parks no person shall deposit litter in any park within the city except in receptacles and in such a manner that the litter will be prevented from being carried or deposited by the elements upon any part of the park or upon any other public place or private premises where receptacles are not provided all such litter shall be removed from the park by the person responsible for its presence and properly disposed of elsewhere in a lawful manner 08   litter at construction sites  loading and unloading docks a each contractor shall be responsible for the job site so that litter will be prevented from being carried or deposited by the elements upon any public place or other private premises b litter or other debris including dirt and mud deposited as the result of normal construction process upon any public place or private premises shall be removed by the contractor c the person owning operating or in control of a loading or unloading dock shall maintain private receptacles for collection of litter and shall at all times maintain the dock area free of litter in such a manner that litter will be prevented from being carried or deposited by the elements upon any public place or other private premises 09   parking lots a litter receptacles required any public place or private premises containing any provision for parking vehicles shall be equipped with litter receptacles in compliance with this section such premises shall include but not be limited to such places as shopping centers outdoor theaters drivein restaurants gasoline service stations apartment developments parking lots and any other place where provision is made for vehicles to stop or park in a designated area for any purpose b number of receptacles all premises having parking lots shall provide in an easily accessible location a minimum of one refuse container for every 50 parking spaces c specifications litter receptacles shall have tight fitting lids or tops and shall be weighted or attached to the ground or other fixed structures as necessary to prevent spillage a minimum container size of 20 gallons or 757 liters shall be used d cleanliness premises used for the purpose designated herein shall be kept in a litterfree condition and all litter shall be removed periodically from the receptacles e obligation to use receptacles it shall be the duty and obligation of all persons using parking areas to use such litter receptacles as hereinabove provided for the purposes intended and it shall be unlawful for any person to deposit upon any such parking lot any litter 10   distribution of handbills a public places no person shall deposit or sell any handbill in or upon any public premises not to do so may securely place any such handbill in such a manner as to prevent such handbill from being deposited by the elements upon any public place or other private premises except date and time of issuance and the contact information for the citys code enforcement office b a written copy of the stopwork order shall be prominently placed on the main entrance to the subject property or in any other prominent location in such a manner as to provide notice to the owner of the property along with any contractors subcontractors agents or employees thereof that while the stopwork order is in place it shall be illegal for any further new construction alteration demolition or installation to proceed on the property c the stopwork order shall remain in effect until it is either 1 lifted by the citys code enforcement office or city manager  2 the violation is remedied to the satisfaction of the code enforcement office or city manager  or 3 the matter is appealed to the city council and following a hearing the city council lifts the stopwork order d a stopwork order may be appealed to the city council upon written notice of appeal delivered to the citys code enforcement office or to the city manager the recipient of such appeal shall submit such to the city secretary for inclusion on the next regularly scheduled city council meeting as the texas open meetings act will allow or at a regularly scheduled city council meeting of the appellants choice thereupon a hearing shall be held on the matter and the city council shall review all information provided by appellant and the details of the alleged violation and thereupon make a determination as to whether the stopwork order shall be lifted or remain in force until remedied e a violation of a stopwork order is a class c misdemeanor f each day of a violation of a stopwork order shall be considered a separate violation and subject to the penalty set forth in subsection e of this section g buildings or structures which has any or all of the following conditions or defects existing to the extent that the life health property or safety of the public including unoccupied residences or occupants of buildings or structures are endangered 1 whenever any doorway or means of exit is not sufficient to provide safe and adequate means of exit in case of fire 2 whenever any walking surface is so unsafe as to not provide adequate means of exit 3 whenever the stress in any materials due to all live and dead loads is more than one times the working stress allowed in the adopted thereby injure persons or damage property 6 whenever any portion thereof has wracked warped buckled or settled to such an extent that walls or other portions have materially less resistance to winds than is required in similar new construction 7 whenever for any reason the unoccupied residences or buildings or occupied buildings or structures or portions thereof is manifestly unsafe for the purpose for which it is being used 8 whenever the exterior walls or other vertical structural members list lean or buckle to such an extent that a plumb line passing center of gravity does not fall inside the middle onethird of the base 9 whenever the unoccupied residences or buildings or occupied buildings or structures exclusive of foundation shows 33 percent or more damage of its supporting members or 50 percent of its nonsupporting members enclosing or outside walls or coverings 10 whenever an unoccupied residence or building or occupied building or structure used or intending to be used for inhabitation because of inadequate light air or sanitary facilities is determined by the city operations director to be unfit for human habitation or in such a condition that is likely to cause sickness or disease 11 whenever any unoccupied residences or buildings or occupied buildings or structures because of any reason is determined by the fire marshal to be a fire hazard 55     standards for ordering repair vacation or demolition the following standards shall be followed in substance by the authorized official and the city council in ordering repair vacation or demolition 1 if the substandard building can reasonably be repaired so that it will no longer exist in violation of the terms of this subchapter it shall be ordered repaired 2 if the substandard building is in such condition as to make it dangerous to the health safety or general welfare of the public around an unoccupied residence or occupants of an occupied building or structure it shall be ordered to be vacated 3 in any case where a substandard building is 50 percent damaged or decayed or deteriorated from its original value or structure it shall be demolished and in all cases where an unoccupied residence or occupied building or structure cannot be repaired so that it will no longer exist in violation of the terms of this section it shall be demolished in all cases where a substandard building is a fire hazard existing or erected in violation of the terms of this section or any ordinance of the city or statute of the state it shall be demolished or repaired to the extent that the fire hazard will be eliminated 56   enforcement by city manager  inspections  rightofentry a general administration the city manager or his designee building official fire marshal or authorized letter addressed to such owner at his last known address but if such address cannot be ascertained after reasonable effort notice may be served by publication two times within ten consecutive days in within the city limits but if such office place of business or officer cannot be so located after reasonable effort service may be made by certified letter addressed to the corporate headquarters address but if such address cannot be ascertained after reasonable effort the notice may be served upon the registered agent of the corporation or by publication two times within ten consecutive days in a newspaper of general circulation published in the city 3 in all cases if the ownership of the building is unknown then the notice shall be considered served in addition with other prescribed provided for above shall be addressed to the owner but if the owner is not known service may be had by publication addressed to the owner of general description of the property involved the notice
